***elf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a> (2170)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ellef</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ellef</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ainalif</i>, a compound of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ainaz</i> and <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*-lif</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">alve</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">eleven</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">elleve</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_2">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>eleven</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elven.html>elven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elfje.html>elfje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The number eleven, or a representation thereof.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>Elf</a></i>, itself borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ælf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*albiz</i>. Displaced native <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alf.html>alf</a></i>, from the same Germanic source.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elfen.html>elfen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elfje.html>elfje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">elve</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">elfin</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a></a> (<i>mythical creature</i>)</li>
<li><a href="English">brownie</a></li></ol>

***elide.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:elide.html>elide</a> (83698)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ēlīdō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I strike out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:elide.html>elide</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">elides</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">eliding</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">elided</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To leave out or omit (something).
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1995</b>,  Andrew Bennett and Nicholas Royle,  <cite>An introduction to literature, criticism and theory</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Graham Hough's apparently objective assertion that 'Ozymandias' <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> 'extremely clear and direct', for example, <b>elides</b> the question of 'to whom?'.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To cut off, as a vowel or a syllable.</li>
<li>to conflate; to smear together; to blur the distinction between.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b> July 10,  “Because <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>’re worth it”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Economist" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Economist">The Economist</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.economist.com/news/international/21606872-how-and-why-lofty-ideologies-cohabit-rampant-corruption-because-were-worth-it">[3]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">As Ms Shafak summarises, “the state <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> privileged, all-powerful and yet paradoxically safeguarded as if it <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> a fragile entity in need of protection.” Between it and its citizens a gulf looms; conversely, <a href = vnd.unilang:officials.html>officials</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:elide.html>elide</a></b> its interests with their own.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The third sense, “conflate”, seems to be a recent development. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not recognized by dictionaries such as Merriam-Webster and can be considered to be incorrect.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="4" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">collide</span></li>

</body>

***elk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:elk.html>elk</a> (601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">elc</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">each</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:elk.html>elk</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiwô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ever, always</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ga-</i> + <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwilīkaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elk.html>elk</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>each; every</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The Dutch determiners <i><a href = vnd.unilang:elk.html>elk</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ieder.html>ieder</a></i> are entirely interchangeable. They do not exhibit the slight distinction that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually made between English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">each</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">every</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_3">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a></span> (<span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a></span>)</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ieder.html>ieder</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elk.html>elk</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly in expressions</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> everyone; everybody
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:melk.html>Melk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:elk.html>elk</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>Milk <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> good for <b>everyone.</b></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:elk.html>Elk</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beurt.html>beurt</a>.</i>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ellende.html>ellende</a> (2228)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ellende.html>ellende</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">abroad, exile</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">elelendis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">exile</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aljaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">other</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*landą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Elend</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">misery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***els.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:els.html>els</a> (30582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">else</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:alisa.html>alisa</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*alisu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*alisō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂élis-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Erle</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">alder</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">el</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">older</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">elri</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">elsene</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*alisnō</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*alusnō</i>. Related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ēlō</i>, whence Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aal.html>aal</a></i>, German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ahle</i>, English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">awl</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:els.html>els</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elzen.html>elzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:els.html>elsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<p>First attested in 1607. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">émission</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ēmissiō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sending forth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ēmittō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">send out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:ex.html>ex</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from, out of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mittō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">send</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ember</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ēmer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*ambrī</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:emmer.html>emmer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:emmers.html>emmers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:emmertje.html>emmertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bucket <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">container</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***emo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:emo.html>emo</a> (35183)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Italic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Italic language">Proto-Italic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="itc-pro">*emō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁em-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take, distribute</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, (with excrescent <i>p</i> in <i>ēmptum</i>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">im̃ti</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">имѫ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imǫ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and possibly <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">իմանամ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imanam</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Possibly related to Proto-Indo-European <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*nem-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take or give <a href = vnd.unilang:ones.html>ones</a> due</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with its descendants <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nim.html>nim</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">nemme</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">nehmen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">nimme</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νέμω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">némō</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la">emō</strong> (<i>present infinitive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">emere</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> active</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">ēmī</b>, <i>supine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">ēmptum</b>); <i>third conjugation</i>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> I buy, purchase.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="la">compārō</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="la">vēndō</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="green"><b>405 <small class="ce-date"><span title="Glossary and display preference">CE</span></small></b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jerome" class="extiw" title="w:Jerome">Jerome</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgate" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgate">Vulgate</a></i> Ioannes.4.8:<dl><dd><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="la">discipuli enim eius abierant in civitatem ut cibos <b>emerent</b></span><dl><dd>so his <a href = vnd.unilang:disciples.html>disciples</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a> away unto the city to <b>buy</b> food</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="la">Quantīs haec poma <b>ēmisti</b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">How much have you paid for these fruits?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> I acquire, procure.</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">émulsion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ēmulsiō, ēmulsiōnis</i>, based on <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ēmulgeō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I milk out, extract</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***en.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> (10)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_4">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ende</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ande</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:inde.html>inde</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:andi.html>andi</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂entí</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_3">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>and
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oude.html>oude</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zee.html>zee</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:The_Old_Man_and_the_Sea" class="extiw" title="w:en:The Old Man and the Sea">The Old <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a> <b>and</b> the Sea.</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>well, so
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ermee.html>ermee</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Well</b>, how're you doing?</span></div></dd>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_4">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ne</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ne</i>.
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:energie.html>energie</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">energy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drank.html>drank</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">energy <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a></i>.

***eng.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eng.html>eng</a> (1960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:enge.html>enge</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*engi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*anguz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:eng.html>eng</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">engi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_3">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eng.html>eng</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:enger.html>enger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">engst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>narrow</li>
<li>small</li>
<li>scary, creepy</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>engels</a> (1260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>Engels</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">English</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> weights <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">esterling</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pennysterling</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>engels</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>engelsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>engelsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A unit of mass equal to one twentieth of an ounce, approximately 1.5 grams</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A physical weight used for weighing gold or silver</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">esterling</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
